Explorer was created by Jórdi Fernandez, Antoine Maisondieu and Olivier Pescheux. Top notes are Bergamot, Pink Pepper and Clary Sage; middle notes are Haitian Vetiver and Leather; base notes are Ambroxan, Akigalawood, Indonesian Patchouli Leaf and Cacao Pod. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Montlanc announces the new male pillar fragrance that comes out on the market in February 2019. Montblanc Explorer tells the story of adventures, quests for excellence, challenging conventions and exploring the four corners of the globe. </p>

<p>"From South Africa to Haiti, Italy, Germany or Indonesia; Montblanc EXPLORER invites explorers on a fantastic journey, giving them the opportunity to discover the rarest ingredients and manufacturing methods that combine craftsmanship with the latest technology."</p>

<p>The composition is made by three Givaudan perfumers: Jordi Fernandez, Antoine Maisondieu and Olivier Pescheux. Each of them gave his knowledge and emotional experiences about a particular ingredient. The fragrance is announced as a unique woody-aromatic-leather concoction that combines essences of bergamot from Italy, vetiver from Haiti and patchouli from Indonesia.</p>

<p>Top notes: OrPur® bergamot, French sage, pink pepper<br />
Heart: OrPur® vetiver, skin<br />
Base: patchouli, cocoa, Ambrofix ™, Akigalawood®</p>

<p>The bottle of elongated shape is wrapped with leather-like protective sheath printed with the Saffiano motif. The signature star that adorns all the Maison’s leather goods is made exclusively in Hamburg. The sleeve and emblem are assembled by hand at the Montblanc Pelleteria in Florence.</p>

<p>The advertising campaign was shot by John Balsom in South Africa, and the model is Rein Langeveld. Montblanc Explorer is available as a 30, 60 and 100 ml Eau de Parfum. </p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a Something you should have in your collection for sure. Its really not that close to Aventus, it is a designer interpretation of Aventus. Much cleaner and more mass-appealing. Definitely smell bergamot in the opening, it fades quickly. Surprised that oakmoss is not listed in the notes, because the base to me smells mostly of oakmoss with a small amount of vetiver, that gives it a little sharpness. There is just a slight amount of the pepper too. It is pleasant, but again that is just what my nose is picking up and others may interpret it differently. After the opening, it is a linear and fairly boring scent. I get no more than 5-6 hours longevity, and projection is not offensive or very strong. It is clean, perfect to wear to work, it is versatile. I also don't smell any leather, maybe just the slightest hint of it? It isn't similar enough to Aventus in my opinion, this does its own thing. There is no pineapple and it isn't as strong and smoky as aventus. I also think this is great for winter, and good for all 4 seasons.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2316377"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2316377#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2315847" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I shouldn't have waited as long as I did to purchase another bottle.<br />
<br />
If anyone has an old bottle from 2018-19 that they'd like to part with, please message me.<br />
Any size is fine. Partially/mostly used is realistic in late 2024, just not like 20 sprays left.<br />
<br />
First bottle was purchased from Macy's in April 2019. <br />
Batch 03i36i222, which according to CheckFresh is from August 2018.<br />
Creamy, dry, woody, smooth and clean with the tiniest touch of sweetness, and not from citrus. <br />
There was very little citrus to my nose.<br />
This is probably my most complimented fragrance.<br />
<br />
My most recent bottle is Batch 03n45n283, which is from October 2023.<br />
Thin and almost non-existent. <br />
Sits very close to the skin, not that my older batch was a 'beast', but had way better performance than this.<br />
<br />
Smells more like CDNIM or L'Aventure and has that vomit/lemon/citrus thing going on (which thankfully goes away after a few minutes). Whereas when if first came out, it had more of its own thing which made it different from most of the inspired-by/clones out there.<br />
<br />
My guess is they changed the type ambroxan to something else. <br />
It used to be a little salty and a little sweet. <br />
A little creamy, and smoother than how this more recent batch is.<br />
I'm not an expert on this, this is just a guess.<br />
I'm hoping in time it gets 'better'. We shall see...<br />
<br />
If anyone has an old bottle from 2018-19 that they'd like to sell, please message me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2314687"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2314687#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2313271" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I held off on trying this for the longest time because I saw ambroxan in the note pyramid, but it's really not giving chemical screech like in, say, Sauvage. I see this compared to Aventus and Armaf CDNIM a lot, but I prefer this because it's cleaner, more versatile, and lacks the bushfire-like smoky note of both.<br />
<br />
Also, I don't think the performance is bad. I'd like if it had more throw, but this is more diffusive and longer lasting than you think. I can smell it in the air after I come back into whatever room I've been in.<br />
<br />
If you want a sweeter, muskier take on this, try Perry Ellis America (blue bottle).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2307337"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2307337#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2307333" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2306184" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Nick-Euphonia"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2271678"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2271678.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Nick-Euphonia" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2306184ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2306184" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2271678">Nick-Euphonia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-05">10/05/24 16:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Opening is a strong yellow tropical fruit note (not quite pineapple, or at least, not nearly as pineapple-y as Aventus), and it stays there with a smidge of soft woodiness, from the opening till it fades out at the far end of the drydown. I don't get pink pepper, leather or cocoa at all. You get the vetiver, and ambroxen and later on, and deep into the drydown I get a little bit of clean linen thing.<br />
<br />
Now for the inevitable comparison. It does not smell quite as nice as Aventus, I gave Aventus scent itself a 10/10 this is more like an 7.5/10. The pineapple is not as juicy or sharp, the whole construction is a little more simple and linear, and it just doesn't have the beautiful composition that Aventus has. But as for this compared to my recent sample of Aventus - this performs much better. Projection is easily twice as much, and lasts about two hours longer. Scent maybe gets you 75% of the way to Avetnus, but performance is better, and price is obviously far better.<br />
<br />
This is a no-brainer at this price. It's pretty versatile. Affordable. Pleasant. Can't really complain about anything here. 7.5/10 scent. 8/10 over all.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2306184"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2306184#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2305959" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I think it'd be best if everyone just forgot about Aventus and moved on at this point.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2302587"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2302587#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2301948" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2291912" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Jaime N"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1818218"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1818218.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Jaime N" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Egoiste-Platinum-614.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.614.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Egoiste Platinum"title="Egoiste Platinum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2291912ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2291912" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1818218">Jaime N</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-22">09/22/24 18:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've never smelled Aventus, so my slate is pretty clean regarding any kind of associations with the aforementioned fragrance. This one captures a concept and captures it well - that of a man who explores nature and embraces its elements. It really smells adventurous. And even though you can pick some of its synthetic elements right out of the gate, the scent does develop into a naturalistic landscape with its fresh fruity opening and its earthy, almost granitic drydown. Like a mountainous waterfall surrounded by a forest where the cold breeze and the smell of granite heated under the sun create this very masculine, confident, almost rugged yet breezy and light experience. And despite its naturalistic vibe and rather rugged masculinity, it still manages to retain a dash of sophistication and lightness that really help in the versatility department. It makes a great signature scent and, for what is worth, it's one of my complimented fragrances. A word for those who think this thing doesn't perform - you may become nose-blind to the ambroxan in here. People will pick this up 7-8 hours after you spray. <br />
<br />
For the price, it's a no-brainer.<br />
<br />
7.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2291912"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2291912#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2291798" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2256183">jmendez1159</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-16">09/16/24 12:47</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>4/10 I really want to like this fragrance but maybe it's just my skin. There's a lot I like about it too honestly but not enough to save it from what kills it. Starts off very woodsy-fresh with some citrus. Smells like leaving the tent in the morning during a spring camping trip. Eventually when the citrus wears off, there's a period of some nice woody round vibes going on. But after about 3 hours, it smells VERY musky on my skin. It's not a bad smell necessarily, but it smells like a "Sweet B.O." on me. If you're into that, you'll love this scent, but I wouldn't call it mass appealing. This was bought for me by the person I had been dating for a while and she personally loved when I smelled a little woody and a little musky. Said I smelled like a man. But I would absolutely not wear it on a first date, with the guys on the weekend, while clubbing, or while in an office. If you do wear it, it would be best worn in cool weather such as 55-75f in the spring and fall. Again, it's not that I hate the scent but on my skin in particular, not a big fan, but I could see it better on someone that doesn't hold onto the heavy musky smell as much. Lasts a long time, 1-4 hours strong, 5-8th hour moderate, 8-12th hour intimate. Pretty decent projection, but not aggressive. About an arm or two of distance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2284887"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2284887#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2284173" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Montblanc explorer is a fantastic blind reach fragrance for everyday and casual wear. its a very mass appealing fruity, woody, masculine scent that is very well blended. the opening does punch with a hit of wood but quickly develops to a more fresh and clean profile. Its suitable for year round wear for both day and night but may be less desirable in the winter time. As i said earlier, this is a great blind reach as you can wear it anywhere, anytime. The largest weakness of this fragrance is the performance. Its just really weak and will project for maybe an hour if your lucky and cannot be smelt on skin after 4 hours. <br />
<br />
Overall id say this fragrance is a fantastic addition to any collection and is well worth the price.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2255725"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2255725#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2254744" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2221719">Fragance_Snow</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-14">08/14/24 09:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Honest review (rating 7/10):<br />
<br />
Many people may mention Creed-Aventus DNA when evaluating this fragrance because it has some similarities as well as Armaf-Club de Nuit but ill give my opinion as its own thing.<br />
<br />
The first thing you smell as you apply is a citrus/woody masculine smell. The bergamot disappears as it dries down and you can notice the vetiver, patchouli and woody aspect of the fragance. <br />
<br />
This is a safe masculine fragrance great for office and everyday use. It’s nothing incredibly unique. Last about 4-6 hours on my skin. Projects well the first few hours then its closer to skin.<br />
<br />
Remember that fragrance preferences are subjective and may perform differently on each person skin, give it a try… ;)<br />
<br />
Regards,<br />
Snow</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2248966"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2248966#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2246409" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2239611" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="GiantMoron"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2211964"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="GiantMoron" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2239611ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2239611" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2211964">GiantMoron</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-05">08/05/24 10:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is what people who aren't into fragrances think a masculine fragrance smells like: heavy freshness. <br />
This is a brilliant scent; this fragrance is safe and inoffensive, but still sophisticated enough to pick apart and enjoy. Also strong enough to get compliments, if you desire this.<br />
<br />
On opening, its like smelling the mist from slicing open a bergamot orange and a green root vegetable, like celery. This dries down into a herbaceous vetiver, then a lovely sweetish wood.<br />
<br />
Absolutely appropriate for the office, and anywhere else, any climate, any time of day. This is a surprisingly good dumb grab that I did not expect to enjoy so much. Moderate to strong-ish projection: 1 spray on neck and wrist does it for me. Shorter performance: about 4 hours before this fades away.<br />
<br />
I love citrus, I love vetiver, and I love that this isn't strong enough to daze the senile.<br />
There is something here for everyone; a great starter for those just getting into fragrances as well as the more experienced nose with an established collection.<br />
<br />
Niche elitists may or may not like this; depends on how much you like citrus and vetiver.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2239611"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2239611#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2238843" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's something about the Creed aventus dna that really matches my personality. Holds many memories too<br />
<br />
Talking about the scent, well I've got 2 bottles, 1 from 2022 and one from 2024<br />
Not sure if there's been a reformulation but all i can say is that these batches are the same performance but i feel like the 2024 bottle has the citrusy opening lasting for more time (its still woody predominant in dry down) comparing it to the old bottle, while the 2022 bottle (might be due to the maceration) is smokier more mature and the akigalawood note is the most accentuated note of the fragrance.<br />
<br />
About the performance I get 7 to 8 hours from both of my bottles with moderate projection, 3-5 sprays <br />
<br />
Btw this is a dumb reach fragrance, all seasons all occasions, from gym to office/school to warmer weather date night scent which gets compliments <br />
<br />
The bottle looks really classy and the atomizer is good. Amazing price value also<br />
<br />
Oh yea and the Creed aventus comparison, the 2022 bottle I own is literally 90% similar to Creed, actually finding the Explorer being smoother than the original Aventus. <br />
<br />
Mont Blanc Explorer: personally from my experience and skin chemistry, it's a 10/10, my top 3 fragrance. <br />
I'd say try before you buy tho and this stands for all fragrances, an older friend also has this scent and told me he gets around 4h longevity, it depends<br />
<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2095800">jaywizard</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-13">07/13/24 21:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've been dreading writing this review TBH, most people I've met who are familiar with it love and adore this fragrance, but I've tried two different decants on multiple occasions, and I don't know if its my skin chemistry or my environment (extremely hot and dry) that makes this simply not work on me at all. I'm glad I didn't blind buy a bottle of this, even while being reasonably priced. The opening is so fantastic, and side by side, almost indistinguishable from Aventus, however...<br />
 Montblanc Explorer doesn't last on me whatsoever. Comparatively speaking, I thought L'Aventure's performance was a little lacking when weighed against Aventus (which doesn't have the best longevity or performance on me either), but Explorer, when it comes down to it, doesn't excel in either category. This scent is weaker in every aspect, which is an absolute shame. I love the woody notes in Aventus and I've always wished for something like a CDNIM EDP with just a tad more birch smell in the dry down. I thought this would have fulfilled my woodier desires, but alas, either due to my local temperatures or my body oils, this doesn't do it for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2217919" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="EbagAppez"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1919507"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1919507.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="EbagAppez" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Gucci/Gucci-Guilty-Intense-Pour-Homme-13075.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.13075.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Gucci Guilty Intense Pour Homme"title="Gucci Guilty Intense Pour Homme"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2217919ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2217919" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1919507">EbagAppez</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-13">07/13/24 19:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is another one of those fragrances in my collection that I start to drift away from and think about parting ways with, but as soon as I wear it I am convinced to hold onto it.<br />
<br />
The whole Aventus style of fragrances has been beat to death, which is partly why I think about dropping this from my collection. But it just does so many things very well, especially for the price.<br />
<br />
On my skin I get 10+ hours of longevity, and really strong projection for 2-3 hours. I know this bc when I first wore this to work everyone could smell me and I was filling rooms. That was with 5 sprays, so I know this stuff reacts extremely well with my skin chemistry. I sprayed it on at 6am, and I was still smelling it on me by 5pm!<br />
<br />
This crazy good performance is what makes it hard for me to part ways despite the very played out boring Aventus style DNA. You add in the great price I paid for this kind of performance - $25 for a 30ml at Burlington, and you can see why it's hard to justify dumping it.<br />
<br />
While I feel like the scent profile overall has been done to death, this still smells good, so I will give it credit where it's due.<br />
<br />
If you don't have any Aventus style frags in your collection, and you don't want to pay for the real thing, this can certainly fill that need in for you.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2133626">BadGuy333</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-29">06/29/24 16:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This one...this one. A few years ago I was searching for something that I would wear everyday. Then I was a fragrance newbie and I simply liked or disliked a smell not knowing what is a fragrance note nor which season should some fragrance be worn. I remember walking in a retail shop in my home town with around 150 euros in my pocket ready to blow them away on something that I would like. After trying the one that the salesmen said that are bestsellers and that was SWY,bad boy, some one million I still don't remember which one, ultra male and ysl Y I immediately disliked every single one of them. I now understand that bubblegum sweetness is something that I very very much dislike. Then I came upon this gem. The salesman said that Montblanc is low class designer and try to convince me to search for something else. The moment I smelled it I just knew this is the DNA that I want as my signature scent. It was classy and fresh at the same time and had very appealing sweetness. I paid the full retail around 90 euros at that time and walked away happy man. The compliments were raining from everywhere. Still love the stuff but afterwards I purchased CDNIM pure perfume and the performance just blew this one away. The difference in the two is that CDNIM is stronger and the drydown smells better in my opinion. The drydown of explorer turns very dry and woody with some sauvage type ambroxan. I highly recommend Montblanc explorer for someone that wants to wear inoffensive mass appealing solid fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2203338"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2203338#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2202342" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
The 2023 one is more similar to the pre-F batch Aventus, fruity-not so deep with a woody accord, a fresher version that’s for sure.<br />
<br />
Now the 2024 one is much more Aventus Cologne to me , I prefer this one to the 2023 one. It has that creamy feeling, a bit more sugary. <br />
<br />
LOVING this fragrance, always gets me compliments. ALWAYS</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2191863"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2191863#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2191825" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1904567">hayggel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-13">06/13/24 16:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Honest Fragrance Review: Montblanc Explorer is a decent option for those who don't want to spend money on Creed Aventus. I was very happy with this fragrance when I first got it but after time I realized the longevity and performance just was not there but still got compliments while it was. I would say I loved it at first then liked it after I realized it just was not worth the price. Its just OK club de nuit intense man completely throws montblanc explorer under the bus and makes me wish I did not spend the money on this fragrance in the first place.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2187422"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2187422#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2183521" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2183521" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="BMulroney"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2137435"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2137435.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="BMulroney" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.52002.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Explorer"title="Explorer"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2183521ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2183521" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2137435">BMulroney</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-09">06/09/24 23:47</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Montblanc Explorer is always described as a "dupe" of Creed Aventus and is often judged on its merits as an alternative to Aventus.<br />
<br />
I have never tried Creed Aventus so can not comment on whether Explorer owes a tip of it's cap to Aventus or is a flat-out rip off.  I also also am of the opinion that that some people get too hung up on these kinds of things.  There are so many perfumes being made from fairly similar materials, and using similar scent profiles, that it is inevitable that there is going to be a lot of crossover.  Add to this the prevailing tastes and fashions at any time and you have going to have lots of fragrances covering the same territory.<br />
<br />
Montblanc Explorer follows a formula that is, in theory, similar to lots of other well known men's fragrances in that it combines top notes of bergamot and pink pepper with middle and base notes of vetiver, ambroxan, patchouli and woody scents.  What Montblanc Explorer really nails is the way that these different components compliment, enhance and balance with each other.  The top notes have a sharp burst of citrus that made punchier with spicy pepper, but offset by the addition of clary sage.  Fairly quickly the vetiver and leather notes come into focus, but with the spicy citrus flavour still very clear.  The transition is less of a relay and more like a musical chorus where more voices are added, enriching the harmonies.<br />
<br />
As the dry slightly leathery phase gives way to the rich woodiness of ambroxan and akigalawood there is a hint of earthy depth from patchouli and cacao.  The entire experience is a really great examples of how to make a really good version of a classic formula using the same core components as many others.<br />
<br />
Montblanc Explorer occupies an important place in my collection in that it is a solid, reliable everyday choice that fits in virtually anywhere.  It is available at a very low price and although it is surrounded by more expensive, more "interesting" scents I still use it frequently.<br />
<br />
I don't know how similar it is to Creed Aventus, but I can say that it is everything that Dior Sauvage should be, but is not.<br />
<br />
A textbook example of how to do mainstream mass appeal with lots of skill and finesse.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2183521"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2183521#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2183133" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2183133" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Dolphineater74"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1830757"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Dolphineater74" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Valentino/Valentino-Uomo-Born-In-Roma-Intense-78740.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.78740.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Valentino Uomo Born In Roma Intense"title="Valentino Uomo Born In Roma Intense"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2183133ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2183133" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1830757">Dolphineater74</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-09">06/09/24 13:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance is summery and fresh, it is very mass appealing and safe to wear. Although the projection is quite weak one can just apply more and there aren't any massive problems with it. This is also good as the fragrance is relatively cheap and mass appealing so one must not worry about "overspraying". I would describe this fragrance like a budget version of creed aventus, although all the great qualities of it are not there, for more than half the price I would say its still more than worth it. This has been added into my collection and is one of the fragrances I regularly wear, particularly in summer. Although there are better perfumes out there. which do all the things Explorer does and better, there are none that do it all for such a cheap price. I would recommend this perfume for teenagers and men between the ages of 15 - 35 as I feel it is not a scent mature enough for an older man, wherein something like a jazz club might suit you better then. The only flaw I feel like I can highlight regarding this perfume is that it is a little synthetic personally but from personal experience it is not as noticeable for people smelling you as it is for you when you wear it. Even so it is not as synthetic as other perfumes and I wouldn't classify it as a major problem, just something worth considering if you are planning to buy the product. Overall I would say that this perfume is worth buying and should be in every fragrance collectors collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2183133"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2183133#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2182931" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2136373">UNATCO</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-07">06/07/24 16:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Montblanc's Explorer slams you with it's peppery citrusy opening of bergamot and pink pepper without remorse. To my nose this is the most offensively synthetic part of the fragrance. When you make it to the freshness of the woodsy drydown you'll understand why people like this so much. Ambroxan is a big player here too, which adds it's usual spice and warmth.<br />
<br />
Normally I won't make comparisons to other fragrances during a review but with this one it's hard not to. If you want an affordable Aventus-like fragrance then this is one of the best options among so many others. It lacks the distinct pineapple of Aventus so it's not an exact clone. If you want that juicy pineapple note then look elsewhere.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2181426"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2181426#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2179525" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Like all other fragrances it’s best to smell it first but with Explorer, it is a very likeable scent and is easy to gte away with. I got it for £40 for 60ml which was a pretty good deal. <br />

<br />
Silliage - 4/10<br />
Longevity - 6/10<br />
Bottle - 7/10<br />
Popularity - Fairly Rated</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2176738"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2176738#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2176657" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2143356">FragGentlman</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-24">05/24/24 02:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is an Aventus inspired fragrance and you can smell the quality of ingredients on this. The opening is the best part in my opinion, yes it smells lemony but it blends very well with the background woods, leather and smoke, then after an hour or so I just smell ambroxan from it, it's like all those magical smokey woods disappear and only the ambroxan stays, which is not a good thing in my opinion since I don't find the ambroxan note that enjoyable. Overall is a good fragrance with decent longevity and sillage, can be worn by anyone at anytime and never be out of place because the Aventus DNA gives it that classy feeling.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The harmony between leather and pink pepper is wonderful, and the touch of sage adds a delightful green note. The drydown is woodsy and sweet.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2149339"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2149339#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2149239" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Versatile and long-lasting, it's perfect for any occasion, making a bold statement wherever you go.<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2132658" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Brett_Sinclair"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2091479"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2091479.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Brett_Sinclair" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2132658ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2132658" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2091479">Brett_Sinclair</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-22">04/22/24 10:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>For the price, this is an amazing fragrance. Woody, citrusy and very masculine. It's a very nice, very safe smell. My biggest problem with it though, is the fact that it's an Ambroxan bomb. Not only does the Ambroxan overpower all the other notes, it also tends to make the wearer go noseblind very quickly. The projection and silage is pretty good but you won't be able to tell because you'll stop being able to smell it after 5 minutes. And if you can't smell it on yourself, what's the point?<br />
I wear scents so I smell good to others but also so I smell good to myself. And when I smell good, I feel good. I feel confident and attractive. When I'm wearing MontBlanc Explorer, I just can't smell it on myself despite other people telling me that I smell really good.<br />
Overall, it's good, very good, but the noseblind issue is just too big of a hurdle for me to jump. If you don't care about not being able to smell it on yourself, or if you're lucky and you don't go noseblind to it, then it's a ten out of ten fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; On the first blast of this fragrance, you are uppercut with a bergamot (as in most fragrances) and pink pepper slice of air as the entire mood begins to change. Although I do not personally pick up any leather in this fragrance, I do receive that graceful amount of vetiver which tends to become a little bit synthetic like as the dry down progresses. This is then led into an ambroxan BOMB! To put it clearly you have to make sure that you thoroughly enjoy each of the notes that are said to be contained inside of this fragrance as this is NOT the most... how should I say... Well put together or well-made fragrance that is out there. BUT! it does hold a special place in my heart and for that I can say I am a big fan. You are going to have medium projection depending on how much you spray whenever you wear this AND this is going to be an easy dumb reach during the spring and summer months. Although there are better scents that are out there, if you are on a budget this is an easily affordable and amazing fragrance that will have the Creed Aventus fans kicking themselves over the fact that they dropped an absurd amount of money on that cologne. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2110324" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="docelder"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1924816"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="docelder" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2110324ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2110324" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1924816">docelder</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-31">03/31/24 21:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a more male version of Aventus. I have had decants of a couple versions of the actual Aventus. I have a few original Creed fragrances, including a now vaulted one. I have to say the demise of the brand is palpable in terms of quality and consistency IMO. As far as Aventus itself, the more smoky pineapple forward version I had of it, to me was the best one. The first issue being that it will never be made again by Creed as each batch is different. They all rhyme, but they aren't the same as one another batch to batch. The other issue, it appeals more to men than to women. It does. Be honest. Or maybe, just maybe women don't really want their man to smell like a pineapple. But, I digress. Enter Mont Blanc Explorer. No it's not a direct clone of Creed, but it also rhymes. There is more of a bergamot forward vibe from it as opposed to the Aventus and no smoke. But like I said above, it's more of a male forward version of Creed. The bonus is, if you like this and you want another one, every batch will smell pretty much like the last. So in terms of quality control, this wins hands down. It's similar to me to the Armaf CDNI Parfum more than to the pineapple forward Aventus, though they both are improvements on the OG for men IMO. The original CDNI is crudely harsh at the top and not a direct comparison to either of these two IMO. Of all the "clones", the Explorer is probably the best blended and smooth overall compared to any of the Middle East clone house offerings. It's interesting to see people talk about synthetics vs non synthetics in any of this. Show me a non synthetic pineapple fragrance ingredient. So there it is. It has the Aventus like DNA. It's more of a cousin to it than a brother. It's less sweet and even though women might even say the OG smells better off a test strip, or from some guy doing reaction videos on the street, women will still gravitate to a man that smells like a man in the end. At least IMO they will. Women will friend zone the guy who wears a pink shirt to the office, and they may hang around him after work, but there won't be anything further develop. That's pretty much how I see the OG Aventus... like a pink button down shirt. Explorer is a great value compared the the OG. For a regular guy that will only buy a handful fragrances to wear at any one time, Explorer is well worth considering for daily use. It also has a consistency that the OG could only hope to have at this point.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="2110324"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=2110324#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2110306" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="1066420"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=1066420#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1037086" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1037086" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Santos89"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/883563"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.883563.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Santos89" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Ralph-Lauren/Safari-for-Men-896.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.896.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Safari for Men"title="Safari for Men"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1037086ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1037086" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/883563">Santos89</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-03-02">03/02/19 13:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I find it utterly impressive that 9 years after Creed released Aventus, it still get's cloned.<br />
<br />
Now I guess it's Mont Blanc's turn to clone Aventus. Or is it?<br />
<br />
There has been so much chatter about this online. Most of it is regarding it's similarity to Aventus.<br />
<br />
I've now had a bottle for a weeks time, and am ready to give my input.<br />
<br />
First off, yes it is similar to Aventus. 90% or so. Like Panama Daytona 10, this one shares that same combo of fruits and woods. Where Daytona is fresher, Explorer attempts to be smokier and adds an amber-y aspect.<br />
<br />
I've read the notes list for this, and must admit they don't make much sense. <br />
<br />
This is basically a pineapple/fruity accord, married to incense and ambroxan.<br />
<br />
It comes across as 80% Aventus with 20% Sauvage mixed in.<br />
<br />
On paper that might sound boring, but in reality it's a stunning combination.<br />
<br />
Mont Blanc really understood what makes Aventus work for so many people, and managed to create a homage scent, that still has it's separate identity.<br />
<br />
Unlike Aventus, Explorer is much more understated. Aventus can, to my nose, come across as vulgar. It's the scent equivalent of a gold Rolex. <br />
<br />
Explorer is a quieter companion. It achieves the same vibe, whilst fitting in with the Mont Blanc brand. There is a sense of class to this, that I haven't found in other Aventus clones. Maybe it's the addition of ambroxan, that sets this one apart.<br />
<br />
Whatever they did, I salute them. Explorer is a hell of fragrance, and not just another Aventus clone. It sits squarely between Aventus and Sauvage, and uses the best of both, whilst ignoring the bad parts. <br />
<br />
Great job, Mont Blanc.<br />
<br />
Longevity is quite good - 8-9 hours.<br />
<br />
Rating: 7.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="1037086"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=1037086#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1455159" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1455159" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Dr. Webern"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1421746"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1421746.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Dr. Webern" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Prada/Luna-Rossa-15754.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.15754.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Luna Rossa"title="Luna Rossa"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1455159ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1455159" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1421746">Dr. Webern</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-11-30">11/30/21 15:47</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Some people will tell you that Montblanc Explorer is a clone of Creed Aventus. There's some truth to that, but personally, I think it is simply Olivier Pescheux's take/variation on Aventus without really attempting to clone it. Does it actually smell like it? Kind of. The vibe is very similar, but some things are changed here: instead of that intense, fruity pineapple you get a drier, fresher bergamot. Instead of that famous birch "smoke," there's vetiver smoke. You get the idea. <br />
<br />
Montblanc's fragrance is a (much) cheaper and more synthetic product, but there are some obvious positives as well: Explorer smells more fresh and as such it's a much more versatile fragrance. Winter or summer, day or night, office or coffee shop... it doesn't matter one bit. It's one of those "dumb reach" fragrances when you're not sure what else to wear. In fact, I am wearing it at home while writing this review. Another thing to keep is mind is that Explorer does have the modern Ambroxan-like component (I think it's actually Ambrofix) in the base, which makes it slightly similar to Sauvage as well. But its Ambrofix is not nearly as loud - or as some people would say, obnoxious (!) as Dior's. <br />
<br />
The longevity of this fragrance is OK, the projection is also fine, but nothing to write home about. Some people think it does not last at all, because they go anosmic to it. But several hours later, it's still there. Since Explorer is cheap (you can get 100ml for under $60 these days) you may want to carry a small decant and refresh during the day. Other than that... the bottle looks and feels great (it's very grippy), Montblanc's "Emblem" logo is cleverly used, the sprayer is solid... I mean, the presentation is definitely above average.<br />
<br />
Now, I know some guys are wondering if they should get this or CdNIM; It's really about what you're after: Explorer is less loud and more classy, and it's more fresh and versatile as well; citrusy and slightly spicy, but not too smoky. Armaf isn't a bad option either, really, but it has a much more aggressive opening and lasts longer.<br />
<br />
In conclusion: if Creed was a designer company such as Prada, for example, they'd have Aventus, "Aventus Azur," "Aventus Intense" and "Aventus Sport" in the same lineup. That "Aventus Sport"? That's basically Montblanc Explorer. Everything considered - scent, versatility, price... 9/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="1455159"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=1455159#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent992259" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1067896" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Freshy lover"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1183680"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1183680.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Freshy lover" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Acqua-di-Parma/Essenza-di-Colonia-9829.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.9829.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Essenza di Colonia"title="Essenza di Colonia"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1067896ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1067896" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1183680">Freshy lover</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-06-07">06/07/19 05:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Welcome to planet Sauventus.<br />
<br />
For those of us that either refuse or can't afford to pay £250 on a fragrance but enjoy the DNA of Aventus, then this is a more subtle and refined version adding a generous sprinkle of Ambroxan into the mix that for a self confessed ambroxaholic like myself, creating an appealing fragrance.<br />
<br />
There will be masses of folk that have never experienced or owned Aventus due to its cost and explorer will affordably introduce them into the world of Creed with this excellent and well blended interpretation thats bringing together two of the most recognisable and popular fragrance DNA's out there in Creed Aventus &amp; Ambroxan fragrances like Dior Sauvage and I for one am delighted these two worlds have finally collided.<br />
<br />
With a realistic freshly squeezed lemon opening, fruity and subtle smokey dry down with an excellent Ambroxan base, makes this a very pleasant fragrance.<br />
<br />
It doesn't spray out much juice, so double or treble up your sprays, then the longevity is excellent.<br />
<br />
No cure for me then.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="1067896"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=1067896#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="52002" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>
