    <div class="strike-title"><span>Most Popular Negative Reviews</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
                            <div id="parent1485771" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1485771" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Made by Kouros"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1395030"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1395030.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Made by Kouros" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1485771ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x0"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1485771" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1395030">Made by Kouros</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-01-18">01/18/22 11:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>BATTLE OF THE AVENTUS CLONES! <br />
<br />
PREJUDICE: Aventus smells amazing, could I replace it with something more affordable?<br />
<br />
1st IMPRESSION: Montblanc Explorer smells super synthetic-acidic first thing when sprayed. Then it's a decent aventus clone for a while, but it's quick to turn into a wood scent that's nice but a bit basic and no longer Aventus-y.  <br />
<br />
2nd WEAR: BATTLE ROYALE. <br />
Left wrist Aventus, left arm ACdNUIM, right wrist Explorer, right arm Mancera's Cedrat Boise. Let's get sniffing.<br />
<br />
Aventus is smoooooth... Explorer is super chemical, on par with ACdNIM. These chemicals sting my nose. G-damn is Aventus smooth and soft, it's also more low-key. Explorer tries to be edgier in the opening. Explorer doesn't smell bad, of course, it's copying a great smelling fragrance. It turns bitter wood quick, the bitterness is what last the longest. Explorer is a weaker juice and more fresh than Cedrat Boise. Not as smoky. Cedrat is tad sweeter-fruity. Smooth smoke, highly pleasant. Cedrat is clearly the warmest of the bunch. Armaf is more lemony+dirty and very screechy-chemical.<br />
<br />
Later: Armaf is the strongest blaster, the most piercing one. It gives me a headache and is absolutely the worst one from the bunch, I can't stand it after 15 minutes, some of the chemicals pierce my brain. <br />
Explorer is better. It dries down to a bitter wood scent which is nice, but not much to write about, there are many nice wood-amber scents.<br />
Mancera beats Explorer by a small margin, but Mancera smells different from the rest: it is not a clone, just a similar type scent (fruity-smoky-wood) <br />
I hate to admit it, but Aventus wins this. It smells the best, it's smooth and classy and lovable. It's gentle. Frankly for the price I'd want it to be a bit more potent. <br />
<br />
I blind tested these for the wife and daughter. Aventus won for both of them. Wife's least favorite was Cedrat, "too smoky".<br />
<br />
3rd WEAR: Explorer disappears on my chest very quickly. It's okay on my wrist. I get no leather. Smells just like ambroxan and "a synthetic molecule reminiscent of patchouli with a hint of pepper and fine agarwood". Frankly smelling this on another person, I couldn't tell if it was Explorer or Aventus. But I'm through with it. <br />
<br />
I'm through with copies. CdNIM was so horrible I feel like I'm buying Chinese bootlegs. <br />
<br />
The watch world calls dupes "hommages". Hommages look pretty identical apart from the name on the dial. You can get a Steinhart hommage to Rolex Submariner for a fraction of the Submariner price. It's not a fake Rolex, because it says Steinhart on the dial. If it said Rolex, it would be a fake Rolex.<br />
<br />
Montblanc Explorer is a Steinhart. You will forever wear at it and think: wow, it's almost as if I'm wearing a Rolex. Others will think: he couldn't afford a real Rolex, but he wanted to look like he did. <br />
(For the record, I can never afford a Rolex.)<br />
<br />
CdNIM is a fake Rolex from a street vendor. Twenty bucks, only for you my friend! Yes yes, very real, very good!<br />
<br />
VERDICT: Montblanc Explorer is a nice fragrance that will please many lovers of woody scents. It is a Rolex hommage. If you want "an Aventus", you can buy a small decant of Creed or a large bottle of nice fake stuff. Or try out Mancera Cedrat Boise, that one's not an hommage or a fake. Maybe it's a Tudor Black Bay, a beautiful diver in it's own right. Whatever you do, just don't get ACdNIM.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="1485771"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=1485771#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1230062" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Creed copied Individuel from Mont Blanc and created Original santal. I believe this is Mont Blanc's comeback. "We're gonna clone your best-seller, Creed."</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="1230062"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=1230062#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1110397" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

<br />
In my experience, it projects for about 2 hours, then it becomes a skin scent. Longevity has been a mixed bag. I sometimes get average performance, sometimes get insane longevity (very clearly on my hand after 24 hours).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="52002"comment_id="1110397"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Montblanc/Explorer-52002.html?ccid=1110397#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1691298" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
